### Round 7: Spanish Grand Prix
*Date: 2023-06-04*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 17: Qatar Grand Prix
*Date: 2023-10-08*
